# StrippingUpsilon2BBBeauty2CharmLine

## Properties:

|                |                                                                              |
|----------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| OutputLocation | Phys/Upsilon2BBBeauty2CharmLine/Particles                                    |
| Postscale      | 1.0000000                                                                    |
| HLT1           | None                                                                         |
| HLT2           | (HLT_PASS_RE('Hlt2Topo.\*Decision') \| HLT_PASS_RE('Hlt2IncPhi.\*Decision')) |
| Prescale       | 1.0000000                                                                    |
| L0DU           | None                                                                         |
| ODIN           | None                                                                         |

## Filter sequence:

LoKi::VoidFilter/StrippingGoodEventConditionBhadron

|      |                                                                                                |
|------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Code | ALG_EXECUTED('StrippingStreamBhadronBadEvent') & ~ALG_PASSED('StrippingStreamBhadronBadEvent') |

|                  |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
|------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Inputs           | [ 'Phys/D2HHHHBeauty2Charm' , 'Phys/PiTopoInputsBeauty2CharmFilter' ]                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
